        function loadCustomOfferText() {
            return {
                output: '',
                init($dispatch) {
                    var toolbarOptions = [
                        [{'header': [1, 2, 3, false]}],
                        ['bold', 'italic', 'underline', 'strike', 'link'],
                        [{'color': []}],
                        [{'list': 'ordered'}, {'list': 'bullet'}, {'list': "check"}],
                        ['clean']
                    ];

                    var quill = new Quill(this.$refs.quillEditor, {
                        modules: {
                            toolbar: toolbarOptions,
                            imageCompressor: {
                                quality: 0.7, // default
                                maxWidth: 700, // default
                            }
                        },
                        theme: 'snow',
                    });

                    quill.root.innerHTML = $("#custom_offer_text").val();

                    quill.on('text-change', function () {
                        $dispatch('quill-input', quill.root.innerHTML);
                    });
                },
            };
        }

    function loadDescriptionMailOffer() {
        return {
            output: '',

                    [{'header': [1, 2, 3, false]}],

    function redirect(goto) {
        if (goto != '') {
            window.location = goto;
        }
    }

    if (selectEl) {
        selectEl.onchange = function () {
            var goto = this.value;
            redirect(goto);
        };
    }

    }

<script>
    function dropdownHandler(key, isKeeper = false) {
        return {
            isOpen: JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key)) || false,
            hasTransition: false,
            toggle() {
                this.isOpen = !this.isOpen;
                if (!isKeeper) {
                    localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(this.isOpen));
                }
                this.hasTransition = true;
            },
            initializeDropdown() {
                const dropdown = this.$refs.dropdown;

                if (this.isOpen && dropdown) {
                    dropdown.style.maxHeight = dropdown.scrollHeight + 'px';
                    dropdown.style.transitionDuration = '0ms';
                } else {
                    dropdown.style.maxHeight = '0';
                }

                window.addEventListener('load', () => {
                    this.hasTransition = true;
                });
            },
            closeDropdown() {
                this.isOpen = false;
                if (!isKeeper) {
                    localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(this.isOpen));
                }
            },
        };
    }
</script>
